var currentContent = null;function togglePannelAnimatedStatus(content, interval, step)
{// wait for another animated expand/collapse action to endif (currentContent==null){currentContent = content;var expand = (content.style.display=="none");if (expand)content.style.display = "";var max_height = content.offsetHeight;var step_height = step + (expand ? 0 : -max_height);// schedule first animated collapse/expand eventcontent.style.height = Math.abs(step_height) + "px";setTimeout("togglePannelAnimatingStatus("+ interval + "," + step+ "," + max_height + "," + step_height + ")", interval);}
}function togglePannelAnimatingStatus(interval, step, max_height, step_height)
{var step_height_abs = Math.abs(step_height);// schedule next animated collapse/expand eventif (step_height_abs>=step && step_height_abs<=(max_height-step)){step_height += step;currentContent.style.height = Math.abs(step_height) + "px";var value = Math.round(Math.abs(max_height * step_height / 10000));currentContent.style.opacity = value/10;currentContent.style.filter = 'alpha(opacity=' + value*10 + ')';setTimeout("togglePannelAnimatingStatus("+ interval + "," + step+ "," + max_height + "," + step_height + ")", interval);}// animated expand/collapse doneelse{if (step_height_abs<step)expandCollapseFilter(2);else{currentContent.style.opacity = 1;currentContent.style.filter = 'alpha(opacity=100)';expandCollapseFilter(1);}currentContent.style.height = "";currentContent = null;}
}function showMoreFilters(){document.getElementById("dnn_ctr306650_ViewLayoutManager_SCESideMenu_8_hMaxOptionsPerFilter").value = parseInt(document.getElementById("dnn_ctr306650_ViewLayoutManager_SCESideMenu_8_hMaxOptionsPerFilter").value) + parseInt(document.getElementById("dnn_ctr306650_ViewLayoutManager_SCESideMenu_8_hMaxOptionsPerFilter").value)createFilters();}function createFilters(){if (document.getElementById("sortFilters") && document.getElementById("dnn_ctr306650_ViewLayoutManager_SCESideMenu_8_hTopFilter").value != ''){if (document.getElementById("dnn_ctr306650_ViewLayoutManager_SCESideMenu_8_hTopFilterClosed").value == "close")expandCollapseFilter(2);
